0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eYou can load the models using Keras. Below is a Python script to load a model and use it for transfer learning.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"import tensorflow as tf\nfrom tensorflow.keras.models import load_model\n\ndef load_keras_model(model_name):\n    model_path = f'models/{model_name}'\n    model = tf.keras.models.load_model(model_path)\n    return model\n\ndef print_model_summary(model):\n    model.summary()\n\ndef transfer_learning_example(model):\n    # Freezing the layers except the last 4 layers\n    for layer in model.layers[:-4]:\n        layer.trainable = False\n    \n    # Adding custom layers for transfer learning\n    x = model.output\n    x = tf.keras.layers.GlobalAveragePooling2D()(x)\n    x = tf.keras.layers.Dense(1024, activation='relu')(x)\n    predictions = tf.keras.layers.Dense(1, activation='sigmoid')(x)\n\n    # Creating the final model\n    model_final = tf.keras.models.Model(inputs=model.input, outputs=predictions)\n    \n    # Compile the model\n    model_final.compile(optimizer='adam', loss='binary_crossentropy', metrics=['accuracy'])\n\n    return model_final\n\nif __name__ == \u0026quot;__main__\u0026quot;:\n    model_name = 'vgg16_whole_brain'  # Example model name\n    model = load_keras_model(model_name)\n    print_model_summary(model)\n    model_final = transfer_learning_example(model)\n    print_model_summary(model_final)\n\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan class="Box-sc-g0xbh4-0 eRvpKx"><div class="Box-sc-g0xbh4-0 cTsUqU js-snippet-clipboard-copy-unpositioned" data-hpc="true"><article class="markdown-body entry-content container-lg" itemprop="text"><div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Enhancing Tourette's Syndrome Classification via Cortico-Striatal-Thalamic-Cortical Circuit Segmentation and Convolutional Neural Networks</h1><a id="user-content-enhancing-tourettes-syndrome-classification-via-cortico-striatal-thalamic-cortical-circuit-segmentation-and-convolutional-neural-networks" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Enhancing Tourette's Syndrome Classification via Cortico-Striatal-Thalamic-Cortical Circuit Segmentation and Convolutional Neural Networks" href="#enhancing-tourettes-syndrome-classification-via-cortico-striatal-thalamic-cortical-circuit-segmentation-and-convolutional-neural-networks"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Purpose</h2><a id="user-content-purpose" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Purpose" href="#purpose"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">This repository contains the trained models and scripts used for our paper titled "Enhancing Tourette's Syndrome Classification via Cortico-Striatal-Thalamic-Cortical Circuit Segmentation and Convolutional Neural Networks". Our work focuses on utilizing convolutional neural networks (CNNs) to classify Tourette's Syndrome using various brain segmentation techniques.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Directory Structure</h2><a id="user-content-directory-structure" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Directory Structure" href="#directory-structure"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>models/</code>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Contains the trained models for three different architectures: VGG16, VGG19, and ResNet50.</li>
<li>Each architecture has three different styles: <code>WholeBrain</code>, <code>Slant</code>, and <code>DKT</code>.</li>
<li>The models are saved in Keras format with the following files:
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>keras_metadata.pb</code></li>
<li><code>saved_model.pb</code></li>
<li><code>variables/</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>scripts/</code>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Contains the scripts used during training. We employed the python scripts using SLURMs. The models were trained using Weights and Biases, please refer to their official website for further information
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>run_monai.py</code>: This scripts run our codes without W&amp;B.</li>
<li><code>run_monai_wandb.py</code>: This scripts run our codes with W&amp;B.</li>
<li><code>gpu_batch_2D.sh</code>: Main script responsible for running the python codes.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Models</h2><a id="user-content-models" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Models" href="#models"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The models provided in this repository are named as follows:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>WholeBrain_VGG16</code></li>
<li><code>WholeBrain_VGG19</code></li>
<li><code>WholeBrain_ResNet50</code></li>
<li><code>Slant_VGG16</code></li>
<li><code>Slant_VGG19</code></li>
<li><code>Slant_ResNet50</code></li>
<li><code>DKT_VGG16</code></li>
<li><code>DKT_VGG19</code></li>
<li><code>DKT_ResNet50</code></li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Usage</h2><a id="user-content-usage" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Usage" href="#usage"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">To use these models for transfer learning or inference, please follow the instructions below.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Loading Models</h3><a id="user-content-loading-models" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Loading Models" href="#loading-models"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">You can load the models using Keras. Below is a Python script to load a model and use it for transfer learning.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="import tensorflow as tf
from tensorflow.keras.models import load_model

def load_keras_model(model_name):
    model_path = f'models/{model_name}'
    model = tf.keras.models.load_model(model_path)
    return model

def print_model_summary(model):
    model.summary()

def transfer_learning_example(model):
    # Freezing the layers except the last 4 layers
    for layer in model.layers[:-4]:
        layer.trainable = False
    
    # Adding custom layers for transfer learning
    x = model.output
    x = tf.keras.layers.GlobalAveragePooling2D()(x)
    x = tf.keras.layers.Dense(1024, activation='relu')(x)
    predictions = tf.keras.layers.Dense(1, activation='sigmoid')(x)

    # Creating the final model
    model_final = tf.keras.models.Model(inputs=model.input, outputs=predictions)
    
    # Compile the model
    model_final.compile(optimizer='adam', loss='binary_crossentropy', metrics=['accuracy'])

    return model_final

if __name__ == &quot;__main__&quot;:
    model_name = 'vgg16_whole_brain'  # Example model name
    model = load_keras_model(model_name)
    print_model_summary(model)
    model_final = transfer_learning_example(model)
    print_model_summary(model_final)
"><pre><span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">tensorflow</span> <span class="pl-k">as</span> <span class="pl-s1">tf</span>
<span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s1">tensorflow</span>.<span class="pl-s1">keras</span>.<span class="pl-s1">models</span> <span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">load_model</span>

<span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">load_keras_model</span>(<span class="pl-s1">model_name</span>):
    <span class="pl-s1">model_path</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s">f'models/<span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">model_name</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>'</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">model</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">tf</span>.<span class="pl-s1">keras</span>.<span class="pl-s1">models</span>.<span class="pl-en">load_model</span>(<span class="pl-s1">model_path</span>)
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">model</span>

<span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">print_model_summary</span>(<span class="pl-s1">model</span>):
    <span class="pl-s1">model</span>.<span class="pl-en">summary</span>()

<span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">transfer_learning_example</span>(<span class="pl-s1">model</span>):
    <span class="pl-c"># Freezing the layers except the last 4 layers</span>
    <span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-s1">layer</span> <span class="pl-c1">in</span> <span class="pl-s1">model</span>.<span class="pl-s1">layers</span>[:<span class="pl-c1">-</span><span class="pl-c1">4</span>]:
        <span class="pl-s1">layer</span>.<span class="pl-s1">trainable</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">False</span>
    
    <span class="pl-c"># Adding custom layers for transfer learning</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">x</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">model</span>.<span class="pl-s1">output</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">x</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">tf</span>.<span class="pl-s1">keras</span>.<span class="pl-s1">layers</span>.<span class="pl-v">GlobalAveragePooling2D</span>()(<span class="pl-s1">x</span>)
    <span class="pl-s1">x</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">tf</span>.<span class="pl-s1">keras</span>.<span class="pl-s1">layers</span>.<span class="pl-v">Dense</span>(<span class="pl-c1">1024</span>, <span class="pl-s1">activation</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">'relu'</span>)(<span class="pl-s1">x</span>)
    <span class="pl-s1">predictions</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">tf</span>.<span class="pl-s1">keras</span>.<span class="pl-s1">layers</span>.<span class="pl-v">Dense</span>(<span class="pl-c1">1</span>, <span class="pl-s1">activation</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">'sigmoid'</span>)(<span class="pl-s1">x</span>)

    <span class="pl-c"># Creating the final model</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">model_final</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">tf</span>.<span class="pl-s1">keras</span>.<span class="pl-s1">models</span>.<span class="pl-v">Model</span>(<span class="pl-s1">inputs</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">model</span>.<span class="pl-s1">input</span>, <span class="pl-s1">outputs</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">predictions</span>)
    
    <span class="pl-c"># Compile the model</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">model_final</span>.<span class="pl-en">compile</span>(<span class="pl-s1">optimizer</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">'adam'</span>, <span class="pl-s1">loss</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">'binary_crossentropy'</span>, <span class="pl-s1">metrics</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span>[<span class="pl-s">'accuracy'</span>])

    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">model_final</span>

<span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-s1">__name__</span> <span class="pl-c1">==</span> <span class="pl-s">"__main__"</span>:
    <span class="pl-s1">model_name</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s">'vgg16_whole_brain'</span>  <span class="pl-c"># Example model name</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">model</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">load_keras_model</span>(<span class="pl-s1">model_name</span>)
    <span class="pl-en">print_model_summary</span>(<span class="pl-s1">model</span>)
    <span class="pl-s1">model_final</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">transfer_learning_example</span>(<span class="pl-s1">model</span>)
    <span class="pl-en">print_model_summary</span>(<span class="pl-s1">model_final</span>)</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Running the Script</h2><a id="user-content-running-the-script" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Running the Script" href="#running-the-script"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Ensure you have TensorFlow installed: pip install tensorflow</p>
<p dir="auto">Run the script: python load_model.py</p>
